function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }
function err($str) { die("FATAL ERROR: $str\n"); }

@set_time_limit(0);

	err('This update can only be applied to OIDplus version 2.0.0.170!');
}

	err('You need PHP Version 7.0 to update to this version');
}

	warn('Directory could not be created: update/includes');

	warn('Could not change directory permissions of update/includes');
}

if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
	} else if (sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') != '28e998005c50828ec482b0069ebd3578e91c454c') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') !== '28e998005c50828ec482b0069ebd3578e91c454c') {
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') !== '85e84e02754f455e8aa77ec4131721a62a63831c') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
			$tmp = pathinfo('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') !== '28e998005c50828ec482b0069ebd3578e91c454c') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('update/index.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: update/index.php');
	writefile_5();
	if (!is_file('update/index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): update/index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('update/index.php') != '741839ac5c595825e31b9d85d6cea8ecdd8e52f0') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): update/index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('update/index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of update/index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('update/index.php') !== '741839ac5c595825e31b9d85d6cea8ecdd8e52f0') {
		if (@sha1_file('update/index.php') !== '27c60e9234ba459d51dcb4b93b7aa7fb0e3c0cc6') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: update/index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('update/index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('update/index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('update/index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();
		if (@sha1_file('update/index.php') !== '741839ac5c595825e31b9d85d6cea8ecdd8e52f0') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): update/index.php');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File could not be deleted: update/phpsvnclient.inc.php');
}

	warn('File could not be deleted: update/vnag_framework.inc.php');
}
